&gt;&gt;&gt; NOW TO KNOW YOUR MIND. A DISCUSSION ABOUT RECOGNIZING DEPRESSION. IT\u2019S A POTENTIALLY DEADLY DISORDER, BUT THE SYMPTOMS CAN BE SUBTLE SO PEOPLE DELAY GETTING TREATMENT. THOSE SYMPTOMS INCLUDE A LACK OF INTEREST OR LACK OF PLEASURE, POOR CONCENTRATION AND CHANGES IN APPETITE. IN APPETITE. WITH ME NOW IS MONICA CAMPBELL, SHE HAS A PRACTICE IN PHILADELPHIA AND OVER 20 YEARS OF EXPERIENCE. THANK YOU FOR BEING HERE. &gt;&gt; THANK YOU FOR HAVING ME. &gt;&gt; WE WANT TO GET TO THE SYMPTOMS. THE THING IS, THEY CAN GET MISSED SO EARLY. FIRST, WE ALSO WANT TO TALK ABOUT DEPRESSION. WHAT IT IS, AND HOW SERIOUS IT CAN BE. &gt;&gt; ABSOLUTELY. I FIRST WANT TO DIFFERENTIATE BETWEEN SADNESS AND DEPRESSION. EVERYONE GETS SAD. IT\u2019S A NORMAL PART OF THE HUMAN EXPERIENCE. BUT DEPRESSION AND MAJOR DEPRESSIVE DISORDER IS A LITTLE BIT DIFFERENT. IT\u2019S SAD MOOD OR LACK OF INTEREST FOR TWO WEEKS. AND WITH THAT COMES MANY SYMPTOMS, EVERYTHING FROM POOR CONCENTRATION, CHANGES IN APPETITE, CHANGES IN SLEEP, AND, YOU KNOW, LEFT UNTREATED, THOUGHTS OF DEATH AND SUICIDAL THOUGHTS CAN ALSO OCCUR. UNTREATED DEPRESSION CAN KILL YOU BECAUSE PEOPLE START TO THINK ABOUT SUICIDE. &gt;&gt; AND THE WAY YOU SAID THIS MADE ME THINK, DO THESE SYMPTOMS HAPPEN ALL AT ONCE OR ARE THEY GRADUALLY SHOWING UP? &gt;&gt; GREAT QUESTION. NOT EVERYONE GETS ALL SYMPTOMS OF DEPRESSION. THERE\u2019S ABOUT NINE SYMPTOMS THAT WE LOOK FOR. TO BE DIAGNOSED WITH WHAT\u2019S CALLED A MAJOR DEPRESSIVE EPISODE, YOU NEED FIVE OUT OF THE NINE. DEPRESSION CAN LOOK REALLY DIFFERENT ON DIFFERENT PEOPLE. SOME PEOPLE, THEY\u2019RE SLEEPING A LOT, EVERY EVENING OR DURING THE DAY, MAYBE SLEEPING 10 OR 12 HOS A DAY. AND THEN FOR OTHER PEOPLE, THEY HAVE A REALLY DIFFERENT TIME SLEEPING. MAYBE THEY\u2019RE HAVING TROUBLE FALLING ASLEEP, STAYING ASLEEP. SIMILARLY ARE CHANGES WITH APPETITE. FOR SOME PEOPLE, THEY\u2019RE EATING A LOT WHEN THEY\u2019RE DEPRESSED. THEY MAY CRAVE SPECIFIC FOODS AND GAIN WEIGHT AS A RESULT. FOR OTHER PEOPLE, THEY HAVE VERY LITTLE APPETITE AND EAT VERY LITTLE AND AS A RESULT START TO LOSE WEIGHT. DEPRESSION CAN LOOK VERY DIFFERENT ON DIFFERENT PEOPLE. &gt;&gt; I\u2019M GLAD THAT YOU BROUGHT THAT UP. IT SEEMS LIKE A LOT OF THE SYMPTOMS THAT YOU BROUGHT UP SEEM LIKE WITHDRAWN SYMPTOMS. YOU\u2019RE TAKING A STEP BACK FROM THE THINGS THAT YOU USED TO ENJOY. IS THERE EVER A MOMENT WHERE SOMEONE WHO IS DEPRESSED MIGHT BE MORE ACTIVE? MAYBE TO HIDE THESE SYMPTOMS? &gt;&gt; THAT\u2019S AN INTERESTING QUESTION. FO SE PEOPLE, THEY TEND TO GETOVERBUSY TO AVOID MAYBE DEALING WITH WHAT -- HOW THEY\u2019RE FEELING OR THINGS THAT HAVE RECENTLY HAPPENED WITH THEM. I THINK THAT\u2019S KIND OF LESS LIABLE. THERE\u2019S ALSO A SYMPTOM OF DEPRESSION THAT LOOKS LIKE FIDGETINESS, RESTLESSNESS. THEY MAY BE MOVING MORE EVEN THOUGH THEY\u2019RE FEELING QUITE DEPRESSED. &gt;&gt; YOU\u2019VE ALSO SAID CULTURE IS NOT HELPFUL WHEN IT COMES TO DEPRESSION. PEOPLE ARE BEING TOLD TO SHAKE IT OFF, WHICH WE ALL KNOW DOESN\u2019T HELP. &gt;&gt; YEAH, YEAH. \u2019S A REALLY UELPFUL MESSAGE TO TELL PEOPLE WHO ARE DEPRESSED TO JUST SHAKE IT OFF. AND ALTHOUGH FAITH CAN PLAY A HUGE ROLE IN RECOVERY AND HEALING, ALSO MESSAGES THAT WE JUST NEED TO PRAY ABOUT DEPRESSION IS NOT REALLY HELPFUL. DEPRESSION IS A BRAIN ISSUE THAT INVOLVES BRAIN CHEMICALS THAT ARE NOT WORKING PROPERLY OR NOT ENOUGH OF THEM. WE REALLY NEED TO LOOK AT IT AS A MEDICAL ISSUE. &gt;&gt; SO YOU JUST MENTIONED CHEMICALS, MEDICAL ISSUE, WHAT ARE THE TREATMENTS HERE AND DO THEY ALWAYS REQUIRE MEDICATION? &gt;&gt; SO, MEDICATION CAN BE VERY HELPFUL. BUT THERE ARE A NUMBER OF TREATMENTS FOR DEPRESSION. THE FIRST ONE WOULD BE THERAPY. FINDING A GOOD LICENSED THERAPIST THAT CAN REALLY WORK WITH YOU TO DEVELOP COPING SKILLS AND HELP YOU BETTER UNDERSTAND WHAT\u2019S HAPPENING WITH YOU CAN BE REALLY HELPFUL. EXERCISE IS A HUGE HELP FOR PEOPLE WITH DEPRESSION. SO THERE IS RESEARCH THAT CONSISTENT EXERCISE, CONSISTENT EXERCISE IN WHICH YOUR HEART RATE IS RAISED CAN ACTUALLY BE AS HELPFUL AS MEDICATION FOR DEPRESSION. AND THEN LASTLY I WANT TO MENTION, MEDICATION. MEDICATION IS EXTREMELY EFFECTIVE FOR DEPRESSION. SOME PEOPLE HAVE HESITATION ABOUT TAKING MEDICATION, BUT IT CAN HELP JUMP START YOU SO YOU CAN ACCESS THOSE OTHER COPING SKILLS LIKE HAVING ENOUGH ENERGY TO EXERCISE OR WANTING TO ENGAGE WITH OTHER PEOPLE. SO MEDATION CAN BE REALLY, REALLY HELPFUL AND I CAN\u2019T STRESS ENOUGH THAT, ESPECIALLY IF YOU\u2019RE TO THE POINT WHERE YOU\u2019RE NOT FUNCTIONING BECAUSE OF DEPRESSION, MAYBE YOU\u2019RE CALLING OUT A SCHOOL, CALLING OUT OF WORK OR NOT GOING TO SCHOOL OR NOT TAKING CARE OF THINGS THAT YOU NEED TO TAKE CARE OF OR IF YOU\u2019REHINKING ABOUT SUICIDE OR HAVING A LOT OF THOUGHTS ABOUT DEATH, THAT\u2019S DEFINITELY A TIME TO THINK ABOUT MEDICATION AS A TREATMENT MANDATES AND BUSINESS RESTRICTIONS BROUGHT ON BY COVID. &gt;&gt;&gt; MORE THAN A YEAR INTO THIS PANDEMIC, AND THINGS CONTINUE TO EVOLVE. THE RULES OF THE ROAD ARE CHANGING EVEN AS WE GET CLOSER TO WHAT WE HOPE IS GOING TO BE THE END OF THE JOURNEY. EACH WEEK AT THIS TIME WE HAVE TO CHECK IN WITH OUR FRIEND AND MEDICAL EXPERT, THE PAST CHAIRMAN OF THE NATIONAL BOARD OF DIRECTORS OF AMERICAN CANCER SOCIETY AND ALSO CHAIR OF THE GLOBAL CANCER CONTROL ADVISORY COUNSEL. DR. B, NICE TO HAVE YOU WITH US. &gt;&gt; GOOD MORNING. GREAT TO SEE YOU. &gt;&gt; YEAH. YOU\u2019RE PRETTY MUCH OUR CORRESPONDENT HERE. WE HAVE TO ASK YOU DIFFERENT QUESTIONS EVERY WEEK. LET\u2019S TALK ABOUT THE CDC. OBVIOUSLY A LOT OF PEOPLE WERE SURPRISED ABOUT THIS THIS WEEK. KIDS HAVE NEW GUIDELINES IN CLASSROOMS THAT IF THEY WEAR MASKS, THEY CAN NOW BE THREE FEET APART, NOT SIX. SO TAKE US THROUGH THIS. WHY THE CHANGE AND IF THAT\u2019S OKAY FOR KIDS, WHY NOT ADULTS? THE CDC\u2019S RECOMMENDATION DIDN\u2019T CHANGE FOR TEACHERS OR SCHOOL STAFF. &gt;&gt; SO FIRST, MY GRANDCHILDREN IN NEW JERSEY ARE VERY HAPPY ABOUT THIS. THE NEW THREE-FOOT RULE IS BASED ON A GOOD STUDY DONE IN SCHOOLS IN MASSACHUSETTS. THERE ARE SOME FINE PRINT IN THE GUIDELINES, HOWEVER. THAT HAS TO BE REALLY LOOKED AT VERY CAREFULLY. THE THREE FOOT RULE IS ALREADY IF COMMUNITY SPREAD IN THAT COMMUNITY IS LOW, AND IT\u2019S CRITICAL THERE SHOULD BE GOOD AIR FLOW AND VENTILATION IN THE ROOMS AND IN ADDITION, THERE HAS TO BE MULTIPLE LAYERS OF PREVENTIVE BEHAVIOR WHICH INCLUDE UNIVERSAL MASKING, HAND WASHING, CLEANING THE BUILDINGS, AND DOING CONTACT TRACING IF IT\u2019S NECESSARY. AS FOR ADULTS, IF ADULTS GATHER IN SMALL GROUPS, AND IF THEY ARE FULLY VACCINATED, UNDERLINE FULLY VACCINATED, IT IS RELATIVELY SAFE TO BE CLOSEITH ONE ANOTHER INDOORS, BUT CARE HAS TO BE TAKEN TO MAKE SURE THAT AFTER YOU GATHER, THAT YOU AVOID PEOPLE WHO HAVE NOT BEEN FULLY VACCINATED, ESPECIALLY OLDER FOLKS, AS THERE\u2019S A CHANCE THAT YOU COULD TRANSMIT THE VIRUS TO 24E78. A SMALL CHANCE, BUT NEVERTHELESS, A SIGNIFICANT CHANCE. AND THEY ARE ESPECIALLY VULNERABLE. GETTING TOGETHER IN A SMALL GROUP, FULLY VACCINATED, VERY OKAY. BUT BE CAREFUL WHAT YOU DO AFTER YOU GET TOGETHER. &gt;&gt; OKAY. ALL RIGHT. GOOD ADVICE THERE. &gt;&gt; SO NOW WE HAVE TO TALK ABOUT AS PARTS OF THE U.S. START TO REOPEN, WE\u2019RE LOOKING OVER AT EUROPE, BECAUSE PARTS OF EUROPE ARE NOW BACK UNDER LOCKDOWN. SHOULD WE WORRY ABOUT THE SAME THING HAPPENING HERE? I\u2019M THINKING IN PARTICULAR ABOUT ITALY WHICH HAS BEEN, WHAT, THREE WEEKS AHEAD OF US? &gt;&gt; ITALY IS A PROBLEM. AS WE ALL KNOW, ONE YEAR AGO ALMOST TO THE DAY, ITALY WAS THE FIRST COUNTRY TO LOCK DOWN, AND NOW THEY\u2019RE FACED WITH A THIRD WAVE OF INFECTION. THE SO-CALLED THIRD WAVE. IT\u2019S ALREADY BEGUN IN GERMANY AND FRANCE. THE RISK FOR US TO SEE A SIMILAR INCREASE IS VERY REAL. WHEN I SEE THESE IMAGES OF LARGE GROUPS OF KIDS ON SPRING BREAK IN FLORIDA AND CALIFORNIA, IT REALLY IS TROUBLING. EVEN THOUGH WE\u2019VE BEEN -- WE\u2019VE SEEN GREAT IMPROVEMENTS IN TRANSITION IN OUR OWN COUNTRY, WE\u2019RE STILL SEEING 1400 DEATHS A DAY FOR COVID. IN EUROPE, THEY\u2019RE LOSING 3,000 PEOPLE A DAY FROM COVID. ITALY AND EUROPE MISSED ITS CHANCE TO AVOID THE THIRD WAVE. THEIR BIGGEST PROBLEM IS THAT THE VACCINE ROLLOUT WAS BASICALLY VERY POOR AND VACCINES DIDN\u2019T ARRIVE ON TIME. THE MOORE THAT THE VIRUS KEEPS CIRCULATING IN THE POPULATION, THE HIGHER THE CHANCE IT CAN MUTATE. WE\u2019RE IN A RACE IN THIS COUNTRY. A REAL RACE TO GET OUR PEOPLE VACCINATED. WE HAVE WHAT I REFER TO AS THE V-CHOICE. YOU CAN EITHER GET VACCINATED OR GET THE VIRUS. BE SMART. IT\u2019S VERY PREMATURE TO DECLARE VICTORY IN THIS PARTICULAR DISEASE. THE ONLY WAY, AND I MEAN THE ONLY WAY THAT WE CAN WIN THIS BATTLE IS TO GET EVERYONE VACCINATED. IT\u2019S NOT GOING TO BE EASY, BUT WE HAVE TO DO IT. IF YOU WANT TO AVOID A THIRD WAVE, STOP THE PARTYING AND GET VACCINATED. &gt;&gt;&gt; WHEN YOU TALK ABOUT MUTATIONS, WE\u2019RE TALKING ABOUT DIFFERENT STRAINS. RIGHT? WHEN WE TALK ABOUT THE SOUTH AFRICA STRAIN AND THE UK STRAIN, AND I\u2019M WONDERING, BECAUSE WE\u2019RE TALKING ABOUT THE 1 MILLION -- THE 100 MILLION MARK THAT JOE BIDEN REACHED AS FAR AS VACCINATIONS. AS WE CONTINUE TO UP VACCINATIONS, DOES THAT BECOME LESS OF A CONCERN? &gt;&gt; IT IS. THE VARY YAGS -- VARIATIONS THAT OCCUR IN THIS VIRUS, OCCUR WITH ALMOST EVERY SINGLE ONE OF THE DIVISIONS THAT OCCURS IN HUMAN BEINGS. THERE\u2019S ALWAYS A CHANGE IN THE GENETIC MAKEUP OF THE VIRUS ONCE IT GETS INTO A HUMAN BEING. HAVING SAID THAT, THE BRITISH VARIANT IS THE NUMBER ONE VARIANT IN THE COUNTRY NOW. AND IT APPEARS TO NOT ONLY BE MORE TRANSMISSABLE, BUT IT ALSO APPEARS TO BE MORE DEADLY. SO WE HAVE TO BE VERY CONCERNED ABOUT THAT. THE WAY WE CAN STOP THIS FROM HAPPENING, HOWEVER, IS TO GET AS MANY PEOPLE VACCINATED AS POSSIBLE. YOU\u2019RE CORRECT. 100 MILLION PEOPLE HAVE RECEIVED AT LEAST ONE DOSE OF THE VACCINE WHICH IS GREAT. AND THINK ABOUT THIS FOR A SECOND. WE\u2019RE VACCINATING ABOUT 2 MILLION PEOPLE A DAY. SO AT THAT RATE, WE WILL HAVE A LARGE PERCENTAGE OF OUR FOLKS VACCINATED BY THE END OF THIS MONTH, AND EVEN A LARGER PORTION BY THE END OF APRIL. SO WE\u2019RE ON A GOOD TRACK. EUROPE WASN\u2019T SO FORTUNATE. THEY MADE SOME BAD BETS ON WHAT VACCINE THEY WANTED TO USE, AND AT THIS STAGE OF THE GAME, THEY ARE REALLY BEHIND THE 8-BALL. I\u2019M VERY CONCERNED THAT WHAT HAPPENS IN EUROPE CAN HAPPEN HERE. THAT\u2019S WHAT ALMOST EVERYBODY IN INFECTIOUS DISEASE IS CONCERNED ABOUT. &gt;&gt; ALL RIGHT. BASICALLY WE\u2019RE DOING A GOOD JOB BUT WE NEED TO KEEP IT UP
